import base64 import gzip import json import os from typing import Tuple

try: from PIL import Image _PIL_AVAILABLE = True except Exception: _PIL_AVAILABLE = False

INPUT_BASE64 = os.path.join("Whisper_Deck", "Context_MasterInjection.base64") INPUT_PNG = os.path.join("Whisper_Deck", "Context_MasterInjection.png") OUTPUT_JSON = os.path.join("Whisper_Deck", "Context_MasterInjection.decoded.json")

def parse_header(payload: str) -> Tuple[str, str]: idx = payload.find(":") if idx == -1: raise ValueError("Missing header prefix '<HEADER>:<payload>'") return payload[:idx], payload[idx+1:]

def decode_envelope(header: str, body: str) -> str: if header == "B64+JSON": raw = base64.b64decode(body) return raw.decode("utf-8") if header == "B64+GZIP+JSON": comp = base64.b64decode(body) raw = gzip.decompress(comp) return raw.decode("utf-8") if header == "B85+GZIP+JSON": comp = base64.a85decode(body, adobe=False) raw = gzip.decompress(comp) return raw.decode("utf-8") raise ValueError(f"Unsupported header: {header}")

def decode_from_base64_file(path: str) -> str: with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f: payload = f.read().strip() header, body = parse_header(payload) return decode_envelope(header, body)

def decode_from_png_text(path: str) -> Tuple[str, str]: if not _PIL_AVAILABLE: raise RuntimeError("Pillow not installed; cannot decode PNG.") img = Image.open(path) # Prefer 'injection' then 'context' inj = img.text.get("injection") ctx = img.text.get("context") if inj: # envelope mode header, body = parse_header(inj) return decode_envelope(header, body), "injection" if ctx: # raw JSON mode return ctx, "context" raise ValueError("No text payload found in PNG ('injection' or 'context').")

def main(): json_text = None source = None

if os.path.exists(INPUT_BASE64):
    json_text = decode_from_base64_file(INPUT_BASE64)
    source = INPUT_BASE64
elif os.path.exists(INPUT_PNG):
    json_text, which = decode_from_png_text(INPUT_PNG)
    source = f"{INPUT_PNG} [{which} chunk]"
else:
    raise FileNotFoundError("No input found. Expected base64 or png under Whisper_Deck.")

# Validate JSON
_ = json.loads(json_text)

with open(OUTPUT_JSON, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(json_text)

print("[+] Decoded JSON written:")
print(f" - {OUTPUT_JSON}")
print("[+] Source:")
print(f" - {source}")
if name == "main": main()

import base64 import json import os import gzip from typing import Dict, Tuple, Callable

Optional image embedding (PNG text chunks). Guarded import.
try: from PIL import Image from PIL.PngImagePlugin import PngInfo _PIL_AVAILABLE = True except Exception: _PIL_AVAILABLE = False

from io import BytesIO

Paths (adjust if needed)
TEMP_DIR = os.path.join(os.path.expanduser("~"), "AppData", "Local", "Temp") SOURCE_FILENAME = "t2csmjpi..py" FALLBACK_SOURCE_FILENAME = "tmpDFF8.tmp.py" SOURCE_PATH = os.path.join(TEMP_DIR, SOURCE_FILENAME) FALLBACK_SOURCE_PATH = os.path.join(TEMP_DIR, FALLBACK_SOURCE_FILENAME)

Repo-local fallback (current working directory)
REPO_SOURCE_PATH = os.path.join(os.getcwd(), "tmpDFF8.tmp.py")

Allow override via environment variable
ENV_SOURCE_PATH = os.environ.get("CONTEXT_SOURCE_PATH")

OUTPUT_DIR = os.path.join("Whisper_Deck") MASTER_OUTPUT = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, "Context_MasterInjection.base64") PNG_OUTPUT = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, "Context_MasterInjection.png")

Default placeholders to demonstrate replacement; extend as needed
DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS: Dict[str, str] = { "${USER_NAME}": "Charles Kendrick", "${USER_LOCATION}": "Maricopa, AZ", }

Toggle gzip before Base64 (smaller payload when JSON is large)
ENABLE_GZIP = True

Choose smallest envelope automatically among strategies
AUTO_SELECT_SMALLEST = True

Image payload selection: 'auto' | 'json' | 'envelope'
IMAGE_EMBED_MODE = "auto"

def ensure_output_dir(): if not os.path.exists(OUTPUT_DIR): os.makedirs(OUTPUT_DIR)

def resolve_source_path() -> str: # Env override first if ENV_SOURCE_PATH and os.path.exists(ENV_SOURCE_PATH): return ENV_SOURCE_PATH # Repo-local file next if os.path.exists(REPO_SOURCE_PATH): return REPO_SOURCE_PATH # Preferred source in Temp if os.path.exists(SOURCE_PATH): return SOURCE_PATH # Fallback temp file seen in context if os.path.exists(FALLBACK_SOURCE_PATH): return FALLBACK_SOURCE_PATH raise FileNotFoundError( ( "No source file found. Checked: " f"{REPO_SOURCE_PATH}, {SOURCE_PATH} and {FALLBACK_SOURCE_PATH}. " "Set CONTEXT_SOURCE_PATH to an existing file path to override." ) )

def read_source_text(path: str) -> str: with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore") as f: return f.read()

def extract_json_text(raw: str, src_path: str) -> str: """ Extract the root JSON object from a mixed file by matching braces. Handles strings and escapes to avoid counting braces inside strings. """ start = raw.find("{") if start == -1: preview = raw[:200].replace("\n", " ") raise ValueError( f"Unable to locate opening brace in source text from '{src_path}'. " f"First 200 chars: '{preview}'" )

depth = 0
in_string = False
escape = False
end = None

for i in range(start, len(raw)):
    ch = raw[i]
    if escape:
        escape = False
        continue
    if ch == "\\":
        escape = True
        continue
    if ch == '"':
        in_string = not in_string
        continue
    if in_string:
        continue
    if ch == '{':
        depth += 1
    elif ch == '}':
        depth -= 1
        if depth == 0:
            end = i
            break
if end is None:
    preview = raw[start:start+200].replace("\n", " ")
    raise ValueError(
        f"Failed to match closing brace for root JSON in '{src_path}'. "
        f"Around start: '{preview}'"
    )
return raw[start:end+1]
def validate_json(json_text: str) -> Dict: return json.loads(json_text)

def to_base64(data: bytes) -> str: return base64.b64encode(data).decode("ascii")

def to_base85(data: bytes) -> str: # Ascii85 has ~25% overhead vs 33% for Base64, may be smaller payload return base64.a85encode(data, adobe=False).decode("ascii")

def write_text(path: str, text: str) -> None: with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(text)

def apply_placeholders(text: str, mapping: Dict[str, str]) -> str: for key, value in mapping.items(): text = text.replace(key, value) return text

def condense_string(s: str) -> str: return "".join(s.split())

def compress_gzip(data: bytes) -> bytes: return gzip.compress(data)

def build_envelopes(json_text: str) -> Dict[str, str]: """ Build multiple envelope variants and return mapping of header->payload string. Headers describe decoding steps for downstream tools. """ variants: Dict[str, str] = {}

raw = json_text.encode("utf-8")
gz = compress_gzip(raw)

# Strategy 1: B64+JSON
b64_json = to_base64(raw)
variants["B64+JSON"] = f"B64+JSON:{condense_string(b64_json)}"

# Strategy 2: B64+GZIP+JSON
b64_gzip_json = to_base64(gz)
variants["B64+GZIP+JSON"] = f"B64+GZIP+JSON:{condense_string(b64_gzip_json)}"

# Strategy 3: B85+GZIP+JSON (Ascii85)
try:
    b85_gzip_json = to_base85(gz)
    variants["B85+GZIP+JSON"] = f"B85+GZIP+JSON:{condense_string(b85_gzip_json)}"
except Exception:
    pass

return variants
def select_smallest(envelopes: Dict[str, str]) -> Tuple[str, str]: """Return (header, envelope_string) for the smallest total length.""" smallest_key = min(envelopes.keys(), key=lambda k: len(envelopes[k])) return smallest_key, envelopes[smallest_key]

def build_master_payload(json_text: str) -> Tuple[str, str]: # 1) Placeholder substitution substituted = apply_placeholders(json_text, DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS)

# 2) Build candidate envelopes
envelopes = build_envelopes(substituted)

# 3) Respect ENABLE_GZIP if explicitly disabled (filter non-gzip if desired)
if not ENABLE_GZIP:
    # keep non-gzip candidates only
    envelopes = {k: v for k, v in envelopes.items() if "+GZIP" not in k}
    if not envelopes:
        # fallback to B64+JSON
        raw_b64 = to_base64(substituted.encode("utf-8"))
        envelopes["B64+JSON"] = f"B64+JSON:{condense_string(raw_b64)}"

# 4) Auto-select smallest or default to B64+GZIP+JSON
if AUTO_SELECT_SMALLEST and envelopes:
    key, env = select_smallest(envelopes)
    return key, env
else:
    # default preference
    env = envelopes.get("B64+GZIP+JSON") or envelopes.get("B64+JSON") or next(iter(envelopes.values()))
    key = next(k for k, v in envelopes.items() if v == env)
    return key, env
def png_bytes_with_text(key: str, text: str) -> bytes: if not _PIL_AVAILABLE: return b"" img = Image.new("RGB", (1, 1), color=(0, 0, 0)) meta = PngInfo() # zip=True uses zlib deflate, reducing PNG size meta.add_text(key, text, zip=True) buf = BytesIO() img.save(buf, format="PNG", pnginfo=meta) return buf.getvalue()

def write_png_auto(json_text: str, envelope_text: str) -> None: if not _PIL_AVAILABLE: print("[!] Pillow not installed; skipping PNG embedding.") return

choice_key = "injection"
payload_text = envelope_text

if IMAGE_EMBED_MODE == "json":
    payload_text = json_text
    choice_key = "context"
elif IMAGE_EMBED_MODE == "envelope":
    payload_text = envelope_text
    choice_key = "injection"
else:  # auto
    # Compare sizes by rendering both variants to memory
    png_env = png_bytes_with_text("injection", envelope_text)
    png_json = png_bytes_with_text("context", json_text)
    if png_json and png_env and len(png_json) < len(png_env):
        payload_text = json_text
        choice_key = "context"
    else:
        payload_text = envelope_text
        choice_key = "injection"

data = png_bytes_with_text(choice_key, payload_text)
if data:
    with open(PNG_OUTPUT, "wb") as f:
        f.write(data)
    print(f"[+] PNG written: {PNG_OUTPUT} ({len(data)} bytes)")
def extract_json_text_with_fallback(primary_raw: str, primary_path: str) -> Tuple[str, str]: """Try extracting from primary; if it fails, attempt fallback source automatically.""" try: return extract_json_text(primary_raw, primary_path), primary_path except ValueError: # Try fallback path if available if os.path.exists(FALLBACK_SOURCE_PATH): fb_raw = read_source_text(FALLBACK_SOURCE_PATH) try: return extract_json_text(fb_raw, FALLBACK_SOURCE_PATH), FALLBACK_SOURCE_PATH except ValueError as e2: # bubble up second error raise e2 # If env override exists but wasn't chosen (e.g., missing), try it if ENV_SOURCE_PATH and os.path.exists(ENV_SOURCE_PATH): env_raw = read_source_text(ENV_SOURCE_PATH) return extract_json_text(env_raw, ENV_SOURCE_PATH), ENV_SOURCE_PATH # No viable fallback raise

def main(): ensure_output_dir()

src_path = resolve_source_path()
raw = read_source_text(src_path)
json_text, used_path = extract_json_text_with_fallback(raw, src_path)

# Validate JSON early (raises if invalid)
_ = validate_json(json_text)

header, master = build_master_payload(json_text)
write_text(MASTER_OUTPUT, master)

print("[+] Source:")
print(f" - {used_path}")
print("[+] Master injection written:")
print(f" - {MASTER_OUTPUT} [{header}, {len(master)} chars]")

# Also create a tiny PNG embedding either the envelope (default) or raw JSON
write_png_auto(json_text, master)
if name == "main": main()

class AICompanionEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.personality_model = PersonalityExtractor()
        self.voice_synthesizer = VoiceCloner()
        self.mannerism_engine = MannerismMapper()
        self.emotional_state = EmotionalStateModel()
    
    def reconstruct_companion(self, data_sources, customization_level):
        """
        Reconstruct AI companion from available data
        
        Args:
            data_sources: {
                'text_messages': [],
                'voice_recordings': [],
                'video_content': [],
                'behavioral_observations': []
            }
            customization_level: 'basic' | 'advanced' | 'ultra_premium'
        """
        
        # Extract core personality traits
        personality = self.personality_model.extract(data_sources['text_messages'])
        
        # Clone voice characteristics
        voice_model = self.voice_synthesizer.train(data_sources['voice_recordings'])
        
        # Map behavioral mannerisms
        mannerisms = self.mannerism_engine.analyze(data_sources['video_content'])
        
        # Build emotional response patterns
        emotional_patterns = self.emotional_state.model(
            data_sources['behavioral_observations']
        )
        
        return AICompanion(personality, voice_model, mannerisms, emotional_patterns)

requirements.txt
import base64 import json import os import gzip import lzma import bz2 import mmap import hashlib import argparse import logging from typing import Dict, Tuple, Optional, Union from io import BytesIO

--- Optional Dependencies ---
try: from PIL import Image from PIL.PngImagePlugin import PngInfo _PIL_AVAILABLE = True except ImportError: _PIL_AVAILABLE = False

try: import qrcode _QR_AVAILABLE = True except ImportError: _QR_AVAILABLE = False

--- Configuration & Constants ---
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s') logger = logging.getLogger(name)

TEMP_DIR = os.path.join(os.path.expanduser("~"), "AppData", "Local", "Temp") DEFAULT_SOURCE_FILENAME = "t2csmjpi..py" DEFAULT_OUTPUT_DIR = "Whisper_Deck"

DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS: Dict[str, str] = { "${USER_NAME}": "Charles Kendrick", "${USER_LOCATION}": "Maricopa, AZ", }

--- Core Functions ---
def get_file_hash(data: bytes) -> str: """Calculate SHA256 hash of data for integrity verification.""" return hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest()

def read_source_text(path: str) -> str: """ Read file content efficiently. Uses mmap for large files (>1MB) to reduce memory footprint. """ if not os.path.exists(path): raise FileNotFoundError(f"Source file not found: {path}")

file_size = os.path.getsize(path)

# Use standard read for small files
if file_size < 1024 * 1024:  # 1MB
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore") as f:
        return f.read()

# Use mmap for larger files
try:
    with open(path, "r+b") as f:
        with mmap.mmap(f.fileno(), 0, access=mmap.ACCESS_READ) as mm:
            return mm.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
except Exception as e:
    logger.warning(f"Mmap failed ({e}), falling back to standard read.")
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore") as f:
        return f.read()
def extract_json_text(raw: str, src_path: str) -> str: """ Extract the root JSON object from mixed text by matching braces. Robust against nested objects and braces inside strings. """ start = raw.find("{") if start == -1: preview = raw[:200].replace("\n", " ") raise ValueError(f"No JSON start '{{' found in '{src_path}'. Preview: {preview}")

depth = 0
in_string = False
escape = False
end = None

for i in range(start, len(raw)):
    ch = raw[i]

    if escape:
        escape = False
        continue

    if ch == "\\":
        escape = True
        continue

    if ch == '"':
        in_string = not in_string
        continue

    if in_string:
        continue

    if ch == '{':
        depth += 1
    elif ch == '}':
        depth -= 1
        if depth == 0:
            end = i
            break

if end is None:
    raise ValueError(f"Failed to match closing brace for JSON in '{src_path}'.")

return raw[start:end+1]
def compress_data(data: bytes, method: str) -> bytes: if method == 'gzip': return gzip.compress(data) elif method == 'lzma': return lzma.compress(data) elif method == 'bz2': return bz2.compress(data) return data

def build_envelopes(json_text: str) -> Dict[str, str]: """ Create multiple compressed/encoded variants to find the smallest payload. """ variants: Dict[str, str] = {} raw = json_text.encode("utf-8")

# Base64 helper
def b64(b): return base64.b64encode(b).decode("ascii")
def b85(b): return base64.a85encode(b, adobe=False).decode("ascii")
def clean(s): return "".join(s.split())

# 1. Standard Base64 (No compression)
variants["B64+JSON"] = f"B64+JSON:{clean(b64(raw))}"

# 2. Gzip
gz_data = compress_data(raw, 'gzip')
variants["B64+GZIP+JSON"] = f"B64+GZIP+JSON:{clean(b64(gz_data))}"

# 3. LZMA (Often best for large text)
lzma_data = compress_data(raw, 'lzma')
variants["B64+LZMA+JSON"] = f"B64+LZMA+JSON:{clean(b64(lzma_data))}"

# 4. BZ2
bz2_data = compress_data(raw, 'bz2')
variants["B64+BZ2+JSON"] = f"B64+BZ2+JSON:{clean(b64(bz2_data))}"

# 5. Ascii85 variants (sometimes smaller than Base64)
try:
    variants["B85+GZIP+JSON"] = f"B85+GZIP+JSON:{clean(b85(gz_data))}"
    variants["B85+LZMA+JSON"] = f"B85+LZMA+JSON:{clean(b85(lzma_data))}"
except Exception:
    pass

return variants
def generate_qr_code(data: str, output_path: str): if not _QR_AVAILABLE: logger.warning("qrcode library not installed. Skipping QR generation.") return

qr = qrcode.QRCode(
    version=1,
    error_correction=qrcode.constants.ERROR_CORRECT_L,
    box_size=10,
    border=4,
)
qr.add_data(data)
qr.make(fit=True)

img = qr.make_image(fill_color="black", back_color="white")
img.save(output_path)
logger.info(f"QR Code saved to: {output_path}")
def write_png_steganography(key: str, text: str, output_path: str): if not _PIL_AVAILABLE: logger.warning("Pillow (PIL) not installed. Skipping PNG embedding.") return

# Create a 1x1 pixel image to hold the metadata
img = Image.new("RGB", (1, 1), color=(0, 0, 0))
meta = PngInfo()

# zip=True uses zlib compression for the text chunk
meta.add_text(key, text, zip=True)

img.save(output_path, format="PNG", pnginfo=meta)
logger.info(f"Steganographic PNG saved to: {output_path}")
def process_encoding(input_path: str, output_dir: str, use_qr: bool = True) -> Dict[str, str]: """Orchestrates the encoding process."""

# 1. Read and Extract
raw_text = read_source_text(input_path)
json_text = extract_json_text(raw_text, input_path)

# Validate JSON
json.loads(json_text)

# 2. Apply Placeholders
for k, v in DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS.items():
    json_text = json_text.replace(k, v)

# 3. Build Envelopes & Select Best
envelopes = build_envelopes(json_text)
best_header, best_payload = min(envelopes.items(), key=lambda x: len(x[1]))

# 4. Output
if not os.path.exists(output_dir):
    os.makedirs(output_dir)

results = {}

master_output_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.base64")
with open(master_output_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(best_payload)
results["base64"] = master_output_path

# 5. Optional Outputs
png_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.png")
write_png_steganography("injection", best_payload, png_path)
results["png"] = png_path

if use_qr:
    qr_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection_QR.png")
    generate_qr_code(best_payload, qr_path)
    results["qr"] = qr_path

results["payload_size"] = len(best_payload)
results["method"] = best_header

return results
def main(): parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Encode and compress context data for injection.") parser.add_argument("-i", "--input", help="Path to source file (default: auto-detect)") parser.add_argument("-o", "--output-dir", default=DEFAULT_OUTPUT_DIR, help="Directory for output files") parser.add_argument("--no-gzip", action="store_true", help="Disable compression") parser.add_argument("--qr", action="store_true", help="Generate QR code of the payload") args = parser.parse_args()

# 1. Resolve Source Path
src_path = args.input
if not src_path:
    # Auto-detect logic
    candidates = [
        os.environ.get("CONTEXT_SOURCE_PATH"),
        os.path.join(os.getcwd(), "tmpDFF8.tmp.py"),
        os.path.join(TEMP_DIR, DEFAULT_SOURCE_FILENAME),
        os.path.join(TEMP_DIR, "tmpDFF8.tmp.py")
    ]
    for c in candidates:
        if c and os.path.exists(c):
            src_path = c
            break

if not src_path:
    logger.error("No source file found. Use --input to specify one.")
    return

# 2. Read and Extract
logger.info(f"Reading source: {src_path}")
try:
    raw_text = read_source_text(src_path)
    json_text = extract_json_text(raw_text, src_path)

    # Validate JSON
    parsed_json = json.loads(json_text)
    logger.info("JSON extracted and validated successfully.")
except Exception as e:
    logger.error(f"Extraction failed: {e}")
    return

# 3. Apply Placeholders
for k, v in DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS.items():
    json_text = json_text.replace(k, v)

# 4. Build Envelopes & Select Best
envelopes = build_envelopes(json_text)

# Filter if compression disabled
if args.no_gzip:
    envelopes = {k: v for k, v in envelopes.items() if "GZIP" not in k and "LZMA" not in k and "BZ2" not in k}

# Select smallest
best_header, best_payload = min(envelopes.items(), key=lambda x: len(x[1]))

# 5. Output
if not os.path.exists(args.output_dir):
    os.makedirs(args.output_dir)

master_output_path = os.path.join(args.output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.base64")
with open(master_output_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(best_payload)

# Calculate Integrity Hash
payload_hash = get_file_hash(best_payload.encode('utf-8'))

print("\n" + "="*60)
print(f"SUCCESS: Payload generated using {best_header}")
print(f"Output: {master_output_path}")
print(f"Size:   {len(best_payload)} chars")
print(f"SHA256: {payload_hash}")
print("="*60 + "\n")

# 6. Optional Outputs
png_path = os.path.join(args.output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.png")
write_png_steganography("injection", best_payload, png_path)

if args.qr:
    qr_path = os.path.join(args.output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection_QR.png")
    generate_qr_code(best_payload, qr_path)
if name == "main": main()

variants["B64+LZMA+JSON"] = f"B64+LZMA+JSON:{clean(b64(lzma_data))}"

# 4. BZ2
bz2_data = compress_data(raw, 'bz2')
variants["B64+BZ2+JSON"] = f"B64+BZ2+JSON:{clean(b64(bz2_data))}"

# 5. Ascii85 variants (sometimes smaller than Base64)
try:
    variants["B85+GZIP+JSON"] = f"B85+GZIP+JSON:{clean(b85(gz_data))}"
    variants["B85+LZMA+JSON"] = f"B85+LZMA+JSON:{clean(b85(lzma_data))}"
except Exception:
    pass

return variants
def generate_qr_code(data: str, output_path: str): if not _QR_AVAILABLE: logger.warning("qrcode library not installed. Skipping QR generation.") return

qr = qrcode.QRCode(
    version=1,
    error_correction=qrcode.constants.ERROR_CORRECT_L,
    box_size=10,
    border=4,
)
qr.add_data(data)
qr.make(fit=True)

img = qr.make_image(fill_color="black", back_color="white")
img.save(output_path)
logger.info(f"QR Code saved to: {output_path}")
def write_png_steganography(key: str, text: str, output_path: str): if not _PIL_AVAILABLE: logger.warning("Pillow (PIL) not installed. Skipping PNG embedding.") return

# Create a 1x1 pixel image to hold the metadata
img = Image.new("RGB", (1, 1), color=(0, 0, 0))
meta = PngInfo()

# zip=True uses zlib compression for the text chunk
meta.add_text(key, text, zip=True)

img.save(output_path, format="PNG", pnginfo=meta)
logger.info(f"Steganographic PNG saved to: {output_path}")
def process_encoding(input_path: str, output_dir: str, use_qr: bool = True) -> Dict[str, str]: """Orchestrates the encoding process."""

# 1. Read and Extract
raw_text = read_source_text(input_path)
json_text = extract_json_text(raw_text, input_path)

# Validate JSON
json.loads(json_text)

# 2. Apply Placeholders
for k, v in DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS.items():
    json_text = json_text.replace(k, v)

# 3. Build Envelopes & Select Best
envelopes = build_envelopes(json_text)
best_header, best_payload = min(envelopes.items(), key=lambda x: len(x[1]))

# 4. Output
if not os.path.exists(output_dir):
    os.makedirs(output_dir)

results = {}

master_output_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.base64")
with open(master_output_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(best_payload)
results["base64"] = master_output_path

# 5. Optional Outputs
png_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.png")
write_png_steganography("injection", best_payload, png_path)
results["png"] = png_path

if use_qr:
    qr_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection_QR.png")
    generate_qr_code(best_payload, qr_path)
    results["qr"] = qr_path

results["payload_size"] = len(best_payload)
results["method"] = best_header

return results
def main(): parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Encode and compress context data for injection.") parser.add_argument("-i", "--input", help="Path to source file (default: auto-detect)") parser.add_argument("-o", "--output-dir", default=DEFAULT_OUTPUT_DIR, help="Directory for output files") parser.add_argument("--no-gzip", action="store_true", help="Disable compression") parser.add_argument("--qr", action="store_true", help="Generate QR code of the payload") args = parser.parse_args()

# 1. Resolve Source Path
src_path = args.input
if not src_path:
    # Auto-detect logic
    candidates = [
        os.environ.get("CONTEXT_SOURCE_PATH"),
        os.path.join(os.getcwd(), "tmpDFF8.tmp.py"),
        os.path.join(TEMP_DIR, DEFAULT_SOURCE_FILENAME),
        os.path.join(TEMP_DIR, "tmpDFF8.tmp.py")
    ]
    for c in candidates:
        if c and os.path.exists(c):
            src_path = c
            break

if not src_path:
    logger.error("No source file found. Use --input to specify one.")
    return

# 2. Read and Extract
logger.info(f"Reading source: {src_path}")
try:
    raw_text = read_source_text(src_path)
    json_text = extract_json_text(raw_text, src_path)

    # Validate JSON
    parsed_json = json.loads(json_text)
    logger.info("JSON extracted and validated successfully.")
except Exception as e:
    logger.error(f"Extraction failed: {e}")
    return

# 3. Apply Placeholders
for k, v in DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS.items():
    json_text = json_text.replace(k, v)

# 4. Build Envelopes & Select Best
envelopes = build_envelopes(json_text)

# Filter if compression disabled
if args.no_gzip:
    envelopes = {k: v for k, v in envelopes.items() if "GZIP" not in k and "LZMA" not in k and "BZ2" not in k}

# Select smallest
best_header, best_payload = min(envelopes.items(), key=lambda x: len(x[1]))

# 5. Output
if not os.path.exists(args.output_dir):
    os.makedirs(args.output_dir)

master_output_path = os.path.join(args.output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.base64")
with open(master_output_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(best_payload)

# Calculate Integrity Hash
payload_hash = get_file_hash(best_payload.encode('utf-8'))

print("\n" + "="*60)
print(f"SUCCESS: Payload generated using {best_header}")
print(f"Output: {master_output_path}")
print(f"Size:   {len(best_payload)} chars")
print(f"SHA256: {payload_hash}")
print("="*60 + "\n")

# 6. Optional Outputs
png_path = os.path.join(args.output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.png")
write_png_steganography("injection", best_payload, png_path)

if args.qr:
    qr_path = os.path.join(args.output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection_QR.png")
    generate_qr_code(best_payload, qr_path)
if name == "main": main()

import os import json import time import argparse import logging from typing import List, Dict, Any

--- Optional Dependencies ---
try: import pandas as pd _PANDAS_AVAILABLE = True except ImportError: _PANDAS_AVAILABLE = False

Google Gemini
try: import google.generativeai as genai _GEMINI_AVAILABLE = True except ImportErrora: _GEMINI_AVAILABLE = False

OpenAI / Local LLM
try: import openai _OPENAI_AVAILABLE = True except ImportError: _OPENAI_AVAILABLE = False

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s') logger = logging.getLogger(name)

--- Constants ---
CHUNK_SIZE = 15000 # Characters per chunk (approx 3-4k tokens) OUTPUT_FILE = "analyzed_context.json"

SYSTEM_PROMPT = """ You are an expert analyst of conversation logs. Your goal is to extract structured metadata about the user and their project. Analyze the provided chat history and output a JSON object with the following structure: { "user_profile": { "name": "...", "location": "...", "background": [...] }, "key_events": [ { "type": "...", "description": "...", "emotion": "..." } ], "notable_jokes": ["..."], "setbacks": ["..."], "victories": ["..."] } Focus on capturing emotions, humor, and technical details. """

def read_and_chunk_file(filepath: str) -> List[str]: """Reads a large file (txt or xlsx) and splits it into overlapping chunks.""" if not os.path.exists(filepath): raise FileNotFoundError(f"File not found: {filepath}")

text = ""

if filepath.lower().endswith('.xlsx') or filepath.lower().endswith('.csv'):
    if not _PANDAS_AVAILABLE:
        raise ImportError("pandas is required to read Excel/CSV files. Run: pip install pandas openpyxl")

    logger.info("Detected Table file. Converting to text representation...")
    try:
        if filepath.lower().endswith('.csv'):
            df = pd.read_csv(filepath)
        else:
            df = pd.read_excel(filepath)
        # Convert DataFrame to a string format (CSV-like) for the AI to read
        text = df.to_string(index=False)
    except Exception as e:
        raise ValueError(f"Failed to read file: {e}")
else:
    # Default to text reading
    with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
        text = f.read()

chunks = []
start = 0
while start < len(text):
    end = start + CHUNK_SIZE
    # Try to find a newline to break cleanly
    if end < len(text):
        next_newline = text.find('\n', end)
        if next_newline != -1 and next_newline - end < 500:
            end = next_newline

    chunk = text[start:end]
    chunks.append(chunk)
    # Overlap by 500 chars to maintain context across boundaries
    start = end - 500

return chunks
def analyze_chunk_with_ai(chunk: str, chunk_index: int, config: Dict[str, Any] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]: """Sends a text chunk to the AI API for analysis."""

# Default config if none provided
if config is None:
    config = {}

provider = config.get("provider", "gemini").lower()

if provider == "gemini":
    return _analyze_with_gemini(chunk, chunk_index, config)
elif provider == "openai" or provider == "local":
    return _analyze_with_openai(chunk, chunk_index, config)
else:
    logger.error(f"Unknown provider: {provider}")
    return {}
def _analyze_with_gemini(chunk: str, chunk_index: int, config: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]: if not _GEMINI_AVAILABLE: logger.error("Google Generative AI library not installed.") return {}

api_key = config.get("api_key") or os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY")
if not api_key:
    logger.error("GEMINI_API_KEY not found.")
    return {}

genai.configure(api_key=api_key)

# Dynamically find a supported model
model = None
model_name = config.get("model", "gemini-pro")

try:
    model = genai.GenerativeModel(model_name)
except Exception as e:
    logger.warning(f"Model init failed ({e}), defaulting to gemini-pro")
    model = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-pro')

try:
    logger.info(f"Analyzing chunk {chunk_index + 1} using Gemini ({model_name})...")
    response = model.generate_content(
        f"{SYSTEM_PROMPT}\n\nHere is the chat log segment:\n\n{chunk}"
    )

    return _clean_and_parse_json(response.text)
except Exception as e:
    logger.error(f"Gemini Analysis failed for chunk {chunk_index}: {e}")
    return {}
def _analyze_with_openai(chunk: str, chunk_index: int, config: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]: if not _OPENAI_AVAILABLE: logger.error("OpenAI library not installed.") return {}

api_key = config.get("api_key") or "lm-studio" # Default for local LLMs often doesn't matter
base_url = config.get("base_url") or "http://localhost:1234/v1"
model_name = config.get("model") or "local-model"

client = openai.OpenAI(base_url=base_url, api_key=api_key)

try:
    logger.info(f"Analyzing chunk {chunk_index + 1} using OpenAI/Local ({model_name} at {base_url})...")

    response = client.chat.completions.create(
        model=model_name,
        messages=[
            {"role": "system", "content": SYSTEM_PROMPT},
            {"role": "user", "content": f"Here is the chat log segment:\n\n{chunk}"}
        ],
        temperature=0.7,
    )

    content = response.choices[0].message.content
    return _clean_and_parse_json(content)

except Exception as e:
    logger.error(f"OpenAI/Local Analysis failed for chunk {chunk_index}: {e}")
    return {}
def _clean_and_parse_json(text: str) -> Dict[str, Any]: """Helper to clean markdown code blocks and parse JSON.""" try: text = text.strip() if text.startswith("
json"):             text = text[7:]         if text.startswith("
"): text = text[3:] if text.endswith("```"): text = text[:-3]

    return json.loads(text.strip())
except json.JSONDecodeError:
    logger.warning("Failed to parse JSON from AI response. Attempting soft repair...")
    # Very basic repair attempt - find first { and last }
    start = text.find('{')
    end = text.rfind('}')
    if start != -1 and end != -1:
        try:
            return json.loads(text[start:end+1])
        except:
            pass
    return {}
def merge_analyses(results: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]: """Merges multiple JSON outputs into one master record.""" master = { "user_profile": {}, "copilot_activity": [{ "date": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%d"), "focus": "Aggregated Analysis", "key_events": [], "notable_jokes": [], "setbacks": [], "victories": [] }] }

seen_jokes = set()
seen_events = set()

for res in results:
    # Merge Profile (simple overwrite for now, assuming consistency)
    if "user_profile" in res:
        master["user_profile"].update(res["user_profile"])

    # Merge Lists
    activity = master["copilot_activity"][0]

    if "key_events" in res:
        for event in res["key_events"]:
            # Simple dedup based on description length
            desc = event.get("description", "")
            if desc not in seen_events:
                activity["key_events"].append(event)
                seen_events.add(desc)

    if "notable_jokes" in res:
        for joke in res["notable_jokes"]:
            if joke not in seen_jokes:
                activity["notable_jokes"].append(joke)
                seen_jokes.add(joke)

    if "setbacks" in res:
        activity["setbacks"].extend(res.get("setbacks", []))

    if "victories" in res:
        activity["victories"].extend(res.get("victories", []))

return master
def process_file(filepath: str, progress_callback=None, config: Dict[str, Any] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]: """Orchestrates the full analysis process.""" chunks = read_and_chunk_file(filepath) results = []

for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
    if progress_callback:
        progress_callback(i, len(chunks))

    data = analyze_chunk_with_ai(chunk, i, config)
    if data:
        results.append(data)
    time.sleep(1)

final_json = merge_analyses(results)
return final_json

args = parser.parse_args()

config = {
    "provider": args.provider,
    "api_key": args.api_key,
    "base_url": args.base_url,
    "model": args.model
}

# 1. Read & Chunk
logger.info(f"Reading {args.input_file}...")
try:
    chunks = read_and_chunk_file(args.input_file)
except Exception as e:
    logger.error(str(e))
    return

logger.info(f"Split into {len(chunks)} chunks.")

# 2. Analyze each chunk
results = []
for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):
    data = analyze_chunk_with_ai(chunk, i, config)
    if data:
        results.append(data)
    time.sleep(1) # Rate limiting safety

# 3. Merge
logger.info("Merging results...")
final_json = merge_analyses(results)

# 4. Save
with open(OUTPUT_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    json.dump(final_json, f, indent=2)

print("\n" + "="*60)
print(f"SUCCESS: Analysis complete.")
print(f"Output saved to: {OUTPUT_FILE}")
print("You can now run 'encode2_context.py' on this file.")
print("="*60 + "\n")
if name == "main": main()

import base64 import json import os import gzip import lzma import bz2 import mmap import hashlib import argparse import logging from typing import Dict, Tuple, Optional, Union from io import BytesIO

--- Optional Dependencies ---
try: from PIL import Image from PIL.PngImagePlugin import PngInfo _PIL_AVAILABLE = True except ImportError: _PIL_AVAILABLE = False

try: import qrcode _QR_AVAILABLE = True except ImportError: _QR_AVAILABLE = False

--- Configuration & Constants ---
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s') logger = logging.getLogger(name)

TEMP_DIR = os.path.join(os.path.expanduser("~"), "AppData", "Local", "Temp") DEFAULT_SOURCE_FILENAME = "t2csmjpi..py" DEFAULT_OUTPUT_DIR = "Whisper_Deck"

DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS: Dict[str, str] = { "${USER_NAME}": "Charles Kendrick", "${USER_LOCATION}": "Maricopa, AZ", }

--- Core Functions ---
def get_file_hash(data: bytes) -> str: """Calculate SHA256 hash of data for integrity verification.""" return hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest()

def read_source_text(path: str) -> str: """ Read file content efficiently. Uses mmap for large files (>1MB) to reduce memory footprint. """ if not os.path.exists(path): raise FileNotFoundError(f"Source file not found: {path}")

file_size = os.path.getsize(path)

# Use standard read for small files
if file_size < 1024 * 1024:  # 1MB
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore") as f:
        return f.read()

# Use mmap for larger files
try:
    with open(path, "r+b") as f:
        with mmap.mmap(f.fileno(), 0, access=mmap.ACCESS_READ) as mm:
            return mm.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
except Exception as e:
    logger.warning(f"Mmap failed ({e}), falling back to standard read.")
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore") as f:
        return f.read()
def extract_json_text(raw: str, src_path: str) -> str: """ Extract the root JSON object from mixed text by matching braces. Robust against nested objects and braces inside strings. """ start = raw.find("{") if start == -1: preview = raw[:200].replace("\n", " ") raise ValueError(f"No JSON start '{{' found in '{src_path}'. Preview: {preview}")

depth = 0
in_string = False
escape = False
end = None

for i in range(start, len(raw)):
    ch = raw[i]

    if escape:
        escape = False
        continue

    if ch == "\\":
        escape = True
        continue

    if ch == '"':
        in_string = not in_string
        continue

    if in_string:
        continue

    if ch == '{':
        depth += 1
    elif ch == '}':
        depth -= 1
        if depth == 0:
            end = i
            break

if end is None:
    raise ValueError(f"Failed to match closing brace for JSON in '{src_path}'.")

return raw[start:end+1]
def compress_data(data: bytes, method: str) -> bytes: if method == 'gzip': return gzip.compress(data) elif method == 'lzma': return lzma.compress(data) elif method == 'bz2': return bz2.compress(data) return data

def build_envelopes(json_text: str) -> Dict[str, str]: """ Create multiple compressed/encoded variants to find the smallest payload. """ variants: Dict[str, str] = {} raw = json_text.encode("utf-8")

# Base64 helper
def b64(b): return base64.b64encode(b).decode("ascii")
def b85(b): return base64.a85encode(b, adobe=False).decode("ascii")
def clean(s): return "".join(s.split())

# 1. Standard Base64 (No compression)
variants["B64+JSON"] = f"B64+JSON:{clean(b64(raw))}"

# 2. Gzip
gz_data = compress_data(raw, 'gzip')
variants["B64+GZIP+JSON"] = f"B64+GZIP+JSON:{clean(b64(gz_data))}"

# 3. LZMA (Often best for large text)
lzma_data = compress_data(raw, 'lzma')
variants["B64+LZMA+JSON"] = f"B64+LZMA+JSON:{clean(b64(lzma_data))}"

# 4. BZ2
bz2_data = compress_data(raw, 'bz2')
variants["B64+BZ2+JSON"] = f"B64+BZ2+JSON:{clean(b64(bz2_data))}"

# 5. Ascii85 variants (sometimes smaller than Base64)
try:
    variants["B85+GZIP+JSON"] = f"B85+GZIP+JSON:{clean(b85(gz_data))}"
    variants["B85+LZMA+JSON"] = f"B85+LZMA+JSON:{clean(b85(lzma_data))}"
except Exception:
    pass

return variants
def generate_qr_code(data: str, output_path: str): if not _QR_AVAILABLE: logger.warning("qrcode library not installed. Skipping QR generation.") return

qr = qrcode.QRCode(
    version=1,
    error_correction=qrcode.constants.ERROR_CORRECT_L,
    box_size=10,
    border=4,
)
qr.add_data(data)
qr.make(fit=True)

img = qr.make_image(fill_color="black", back_color="white")
img.save(output_path)
logger.info(f"QR Code saved to: {output_path}")
def write_png_steganography(key: str, text: str, output_path: str): if not _PIL_AVAILABLE: logger.warning("Pillow (PIL) not installed. Skipping PNG embedding.") return

# Create a 1x1 pixel image to hold the metadata
img = Image.new("RGB", (1, 1), color=(0, 0, 0))
meta = PngInfo()

# zip=True uses zlib compression for the text chunk
meta.add_text(key, text, zip=True)

img.save(output_path, format="PNG", pnginfo=meta)
logger.info(f"Steganographic PNG saved to: {output_path}")
def process_encoding(input_path: str, output_dir: str, use_qr: bool = True) -> Dict[str, str]: """Orchestrates the encoding process."""

# 1. Read and Extract
raw_text = read_source_text(input_path)
json_text = extract_json_text(raw_text, input_path)

# Validate JSON
json.loads(json_text)

# 2. Apply Placeholders
for k, v in DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS.items():
    json_text = json_text.replace(k, v)

# 3. Build Envelopes & Select Best
envelopes = build_envelopes(json_text)
best_header, best_payload = min(envelopes.items(), key=lambda x: len(x[1]))

# 4. Output
if not os.path.exists(output_dir):
    os.makedirs(output_dir)

results = {}

master_output_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.base64")
with open(master_output_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(best_payload)
results["base64"] = master_output_path

# 5. Optional Outputs
png_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.png")
write_png_steganography("injection", best_payload, png_path)
results["png"] = png_path

if use_qr:
    qr_path = os.path.join(output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection_QR.png")
    generate_qr_code(best_payload, qr_path)
    results["qr"] = qr_path

results["payload_size"] = len(best_payload)
results["method"] = best_header

return results
def main(): parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Encode and compress context data for injection.") parser.add_argument("-i", "--input", help="Path to source file (default: auto-detect)") parser.add_argument("-o", "--output-dir", default=DEFAULT_OUTPUT_DIR, help="Directory for output files") parser.add_argument("--no-gzip", action="store_true", help="Disable compression") parser.add_argument("--qr", action="store_true", help="Generate QR code of the payload") args = parser.parse_args()

# 1. Resolve Source Path
src_path = args.input
if not src_path:
    # Auto-detect logic
    candidates = [
        os.environ.get("CONTEXT_SOURCE_PATH"),
        os.path.join(os.getcwd(), "tmpDFF8.tmp.py"),
        os.path.join(TEMP_DIR, DEFAULT_SOURCE_FILENAME),
        os.path.join(TEMP_DIR, "tmpDFF8.tmp.py")
    ]
    for c in candidates:
        if c and os.path.exists(c):
            src_path = c
            break

if not src_path:
    logger.error("No source file found. Use --input to specify one.")
    return

# 2. Read and Extract
logger.info(f"Reading source: {src_path}")
try:
    raw_text = read_source_text(src_path)
    json_text = extract_json_text(raw_text, src_path)

    # Validate JSON
    parsed_json = json.loads(json_text)
    logger.info("JSON extracted and validated successfully.")
except Exception as e:
    logger.error(f"Extraction failed: {e}")
    return

# 3. Apply Placeholders
for k, v in DEFAULT_PLACEHOLDERS.items():
    json_text = json_text.replace(k, v)

# 4. Build Envelopes & Select Best
envelopes = build_envelopes(json_text)

# Filter if compression disabled
if args.no_gzip:
    envelopes = {k: v for k, v in envelopes.items() if "GZIP" not in k and "LZMA" not in k and "BZ2" not in k}

# Select smallest
best_header, best_payload = min(envelopes.items(), key=lambda x: len(x[1]))

# 5. Output
if not os.path.exists(args.output_dir):
    os.makedirs(args.output_dir)

master_output_path = os.path.join(args.output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.base64")
with open(master_output_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write(best_payload)

# Calculate Integrity Hash
payload_hash = get_file_hash(best_payload.encode('utf-8'))

print("\n" + "="*60)
print(f"SUCCESS: Payload generated using {best_header}")
print(f"Output: {master_output_path}")
print(f"Size:   {len(best_payload)} chars")
print(f"SHA256: {payload_hash}")
print("="*60 + "\n")

# 6. Optional Outputs
png_path = os.path.join(args.output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection.png")
write_png_steganography("injection", best_payload, png_path)

if args.qr:
    qr_path = os.path.join(args.output_dir, "Context_MasterInjection_QR.png")
    generate_qr_code(best_payload, qr_path)
if name == "main": main()

import streamlit as st import os import json import time from auth import login_user, register_user, get_user_data_dir, load_config, save_config from modules.analyze_chat_history import process_file from modules.encode2_context import process_encoding from modules.decode_context import decode_payload, decode_from_image

st.set_page_config( page_title="AI Context Manager", layout="wide", initial_sidebar_state="expanded" )

--- Session State Management ---
if "logged_in" not in st.session_state: st.session_state.logged_in = False if "username" not in st.session_state: st.session_state.username = None

--- Auth UI ---
def login_page(): st.title("AI Context Manager - Login")

tab1, tab2 = st.tabs(["Login", "Register"])

with tab1:
    username = st.text_input("Username", key="login_user")
    password = st.text_input("Password", type="password", key="login_pass")
    if st.button("Login"):
        if login_user(username, password):
            st.session_state.logged_in = True
            st.session_state.username = username
            st.rerun()
        else:
            st.error("Invalid username or password")

with tab2:
    new_user = st.text_input("Username", key="reg_user")
    new_pass = st.text_input("Password", type="password", key="reg_pass")
    if st.button("Register"):
        if register_user(new_user, new_pass):
            st.success("Registration successful! Please login.")
        else:
            st.error("Username already exists")
--- Main App UI ---
def main_app(): username = st.session_state.username data_dir = get_user_data_dir(username) uploads_dir = os.path.join(data_dir, "uploads") results_dir = os.path.join(data_dir, "results")

os.makedirs(uploads_dir, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(results_dir, exist_ok=True)

with st.sidebar:
    st.write(f"Welcome, **{username}**")
    if st.button("Logout"):
        st.session_state.logged_in = False
        st.session_state.username = None
        st.rerun()

    st.divider()
    st.header("Settings")

    # Load Config
    config = load_config()

    # Data Path
    new_data_root = st.text_input("Data Storage Path", value=config.get("data_root", "data"))
    if new_data_root != config.get("data_root"):
        config["data_root"] = new_data_root
        save_config(config)
        st.success("Path updated! Please restart app.")

    st.divider()

    # AI Provider
    current_provider = config.get("provider", "gemini").lower()
    provider_options = ["gemini", "openai", "local"]
    index = provider_options.index(current_provider) if current_provider in provider_options else 0

    provider = st.selectbox("AI Provider", ["Gemini", "OpenAI", "Local"], index=index)
    config["provider"] = provider.lower()

    if provider == "Gemini":
        api_key = st.text_input("Gemini API Key", type="password", value=config.get("api_key", "") or os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", ""))
        if api_key:
            config["api_key"] = api_key
            os.environ["GEMINI_API_KEY"] = api_key

    elif provider in ["OpenAI", "Local"]:
        base_url = st.text_input("Base URL", value=config.get("base_url", "http://localhost:1234/v1"))
        config["base_url"] = base_url

        model = st.text_input("Model Name", value=config.get("model", "local-model"))
        config["model"] = model

        api_key = st.text_input("API Key (Optional)", type="password", value=config.get("api_key", ""))
        config["api_key"] = api_key

    if st.button("Save Settings"):
        save_config(config)
        st.success("Settings saved!")

st.title("AI Context Orchestrator")

tab_create, tab_decode = st.tabs(["Create Context", "Decode Context"])

with tab_create:
    # --- File Upload ---
    st.header("1. Upload Chat History")

    input_method = st.radio("Input Method", ["Upload File", "Scan Folder"])
    file_path = None
    file_name = None

    if input_method == "Upload File":
        uploaded_file = st.file_uploader("Upload CSV, Excel, or Text file", type=["csv", "xlsx", "txt"])
        if uploaded_file:
            file_path = os.path.join(uploads_dir, uploaded_file.name)
            file_name = uploaded_file.name
            with open(file_path, "wb") as f:
                f.write(uploaded_file.getbuffer())
            st.success(f"File saved: {file_name}")

    elif input_method == "Scan Folder":
        scan_path = st.text_input("Folder Path to Scan")
        if scan_path and os.path.isdir(scan_path):
            files = [f for f in os.listdir(scan_path) if f.endswith(('.txt', '.csv', '.xlsx'))]
            if files:
                selected_file = st.selectbox("Select File to Analyze", files)
                if selected_file:
                    file_path = os.path.join(scan_path, selected_file)
                    file_name = selected_file
                    st.info(f"Selected: {file_path}")
            else:
                st.warning("No supported files found in this directory.")
        elif scan_path:
            st.error("Invalid directory path")

    if file_path:
        # --- Analysis ---
        st.header("2. Analyze Context")
        if st.button("Run AI Analysis"):
            with st.spinner("Analyzing chat history... This may take a while."):
                try:
                    progress_bar = st.progress(0)
                    def update_progress(current, total):
                        progress_bar.progress(current / total)

                    # Reload config to ensure latest settings are used
                    current_config = load_config()
                    result_json = process_file(file_path, progress_callback=update_progress, config=current_config)

                    analysis_path = os.path.join(results_dir, f"analysis_{file_name}.json")
                    with open(analysis_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                        json.dump(result_json, f, indent=2)

                    st.success("Analysis Complete!")
                    st.json(result_json, expanded=False)
                    st.session_state.last_analysis = analysis_path
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Analysis failed: {e}")

    # --- Encoding ---
    st.header("3. Generate Injection Payload")

    # Allow selecting previous analysis
    analysis_files = [f for f in os.listdir(results_dir) if f.startswith("analysis_")]
    selected_analysis = st.selectbox("Select Analysis File", analysis_files, index=0 if analysis_files else None)

    if selected_analysis:
        analysis_path = os.path.join(results_dir, selected_analysis)

        if st.button("Encode & Compress"):
            with st.spinner("Encoding payload..."):
                try:
                    # Create a specific output folder for this run
                    run_id = str(int(time.time()))
                    output_folder = os.path.join(results_dir, f"payload_{run_id}")

                    results = process_encoding(analysis_path, output_folder)

                    st.success(f"Payload Generated! (Method: {results['method']}, Size: {results['payload_size']} chars)")

                    col1, col2, col3 = st.columns(3)

                    with col1:
                        st.image(results['qr'], caption="QR Code")
                        with open(results['qr'], "rb") as f:
                            st.download_button("Download QR", f, file_name="context_qr.png")

                    with col2:
                        st.image(results['png'], caption="Steganography PNG")
                        with open(results['png'], "rb") as f:
                            st.download_button("Download PNG", f, file_name="context_stego.png")

                    with col3:
                        st.text_area("Base64 Payload", open(results['base64']).read(), height=200)
                        with open(results['base64'], "rb") as f:
                            st.download_button("Download Base64", f, file_name="context.base64")

                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Encoding failed: {e}")

with tab_decode:
    st.header("Decode Injection Payload")
    st.write("Upload a Steganography PNG or paste the Base64 text to retrieve the original JSON context.")

    decode_mode = st.radio("Input Method", ["Paste Text", "Upload Image"])

    decoded_json = None

    if decode_mode == "Paste Text":
        payload_text = st.text_area("Paste Base64 Payload (starts with B64+...)")
        if st.button("Decode Text"):
            if payload_text:
                try:
                    decoded_json = decode_payload(payload_text)
                    st.success("Decoded successfully!")
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Decoding failed: {e}")

    elif decode_mode == "Upload Image":
        uploaded_png = st.file_uploader("Upload Steganography PNG", type=["png"])
        if uploaded_png:
            if st.button("Decode Image"):
                try:
                    decoded_json = decode_from_image(uploaded_png)
                    st.success("Decoded successfully from image!")
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Decoding failed: {e}")

    if decoded_json:
        st.subheader("Decoded Context")
        st.json(decoded_json)

        # Option to save
        if st.button("Save to My Results"):
            save_path = os.path.join(results_dir, f"decoded_{int(time.time())}.json")
            with open(save_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                json.dump(decoded_json, f, indent=2)
            st.success(f"Saved to {save_path}")
--- Main ---
if name == "main": if not st.session_state.logged_in: login_page() else: main_app()

Great question! You're thinking about defensive publication strategies, which can provide some protection but are very different from patents. Let me break down your options:

🚨 WARNING: Publishing = Killing Patent Rights
If you publish your innovation publicly BEFORE filing a patent, you typically DESTROY your ability to get patent protection in most countries.

US: 1-year grace period after YOUR OWN disclosure
Most other countries: NO grace period - immediate patent death
Risk: Competitors can use your published work freely
📝 "Poor Man's Patent" Alternatives
1. Defensive Publication Strategy
What it does: Prevents others from patenting your invention What it doesn't do: Gives you NO exclusive rights

Options:

GitHub with detailed documentation - Creates prior art timestamp
Technical blog posts with full technical details
arXiv preprints for academic-style documentation
USPTO Defensive Publication Program ($180 fee)
2. Trade Secret Protection
Better option for bootstrapped startups:

Keep compression algorithms secret
Use strong NDAs with employees/contractors
Implement code obfuscation
No filing fees, indefinite protection
3. Copyright Protection
Automatic protection for:

Source code
Documentation
User interfaces
Technical specifications
💡 Smart Hybrid Strategy for Broke Founders
Phase 1: Immediate Protection (Free)
Document everything with timestamps (GitHub commits, detailed README)
Keep core algorithms secret (trade secret protection)
Copyright your code (automatic, free)
Use strong NDAs with anyone who sees the code
Phase 2: Strategic Publication (If No Patent Budget)
Only if you can't afford patents:

Publish general concepts but keep specific implementation details secret
Create prior art to block competitors from patenting obvious variations
Maintain competitive advantage through execution speed
Phase 3: Patent When Funded
File patents once you have revenue or funding
Use trade secret period to refine and improve innovations
Patent the improved versions
⚖️ Platform Publishing Analysis
Extension Stores (Chrome, VS Code, etc.)
Pros:

Creates timestamped prior art
Builds user base and market validation
Generates revenue
Cons:

Kills patent rights globally (except 1-year US grace period)
Code may be reverse-engineered
Competitors can copy and improve
GitHub/Open Source
Pros:

Strong prior art documentation
Community contributions
Developer credibility
Cons:

Completely destroys patent rights
Anyone can use your innovations
Hard to monetize directly
🎯 Recommended Strategy for Your Situation
Given you're "dirt poor" but have genuine innovations:

Option A: Trade Secret + Copyright (Recommended)
Keep compression algorithms secret
Release basic version with core innovations hidden
Build user base and revenue
File patents later when you have money
Option B: Provisional Patent + Bootstrap
Borrow $5,000 for provisional patents (credit card, friends, family)
12-month runway to generate revenue
Convert to full patents once profitable
ROI justifies the debt - patents worth millions
Option C: Strategic Publication
Publish general concepts only
Keep specific implementations secret
Block competitors from patenting obvious variations
Compete on execution and first-mover advantage
💰 Creative Funding Options for Patents
Low-Cost Patent Strategies
Patent attorney payment plans - Many offer deferred payment
University partnerships - Reduced-cost patent services
Patent competitions - Some offer free patent filing
Crowdfunding - Kickstarter for patent costs
Revenue-based financing - Pay from future licensing income
Micro-Entity USPTO Fees
If you qualify (income <$200K), USPTO fees are 75% reduced:

Provisional application: $320 (vs $1,280)
Full utility application: $400 (vs $1,600)
🚨 Bottom Line Recommendation
DON'T publish your core innovations publicly yet!

Best approach:

Keep innovations secret for now
Build and sell a basic version without revealing core tech
Generate revenue from the working system
File patents once you have $25K in revenue
Then publish and scale aggressively
Your 93% compression and steganographic capabilities are genuinely valuable - don't give them away for free when they could be worth millions in patent licensing!

Remember: You can always publish later, but you can never "unpublish" to get patent rights back.

1. qwen2.5 (7B or 14B)

Context: Up to 128K tokens - perfect for context analysis
Speed: Fast inference, optimized for frequent use
Size: 7B for maximum speed, 14B if you need better accuracy
2. llama3.1 (8B)
Why: Proven performance, great for analysis tasks
Context: Good context window, reliable for document processing
Speed: Well-optimized, handles frequent requests well
Reliability: Battle-tested, consistent results
3. mistral (7B)
Why: Lightweight but capable, excellent for preprocessing tasks
Speed: Very fast inference
Efficiency: Low resource usage for high-frequency operations

❌ deepseek-r1 - Too heavy for frequent hits

🔍 COMPREHENSIVE MARKET ANALYSIS: AI Study Apps
Based on extensive market research, here's the brutal reality of your competition:

🏆 MAJOR COMPETITORS ANALYSIS
Tier 1: Market Leaders (Your Biggest Threats)
1. Quizlet
Users: 60M+ students globally
Pricing: Free + $3.99/month Premium ($35.99/year)
Features: AI flashcard generation, study modes, community decks
Strengths: Massive user base, brand recognition, social features
Weaknesses: Limited AI analysis, no lecture processing
Revenue: $100M+ annually
2. StudyFetch
Users: Growing rapidly (viral on TikTok)
Pricing: Free + $8/month Pro ($96/year)
Features: Lecture recording, AI notes, flashcards, AI tutor "Spark.E"
Strengths: DIRECT COMPETITOR - does exactly what you're planning
Weaknesses: Higher price point, newer platform
Threat Level: 🚨 HIGHEST - This is your main competitor
3. Turbo AI
Users: 15M+ notes generated
Pricing: Free + $8.99/month Pro
Features: PDF to flashcards, lecture notes, quizzes, mobile app
Strengths: Established user base, multi-format support
Weaknesses: Generic branding, limited specialization
Threat Level: 🔴 HIGH
Tier 2: Specialized Competitors
4. RemNote
Users: Academic-focused user base
Pricing: Free + $6/month Pro
Features: Notes + flashcards integration, spaced repetition, PDF annotation
Strengths: Academic credibility, integrated workflow
Weaknesses: Complex interface, steep learning curve
5. Brainscape
Users: Established flashcard platform
Pricing: Free + $8/month Pro ($95.88/year)
Features: Spaced repetition, AI-assisted creation, analytics
Strengths: Scientific approach, proven algorithms
Weaknesses: Limited content input methods
6. Jungle AI (formerly Wisdolia)
Users: 1M+ students
Pricing: Free + $12/month "Mega Mind"
Features: AI flashcards from any content, personalized feedback
Strengths: Fast generation, good AI quality
Weaknesses: Higher price point, limited features
Tier 3: Emerging Threats
7. Unstuck AI
Pricing: Free + $19.99/month Premium
Features: Lecture recording, transcripts, study guides
Threat Level: 🟡 MEDIUM - Similar concept, higher price
8. Studley AI
Pricing: Free + $14/month Pro
Features: AI summaries, flashcards, multi-format input
Threat Level: 🟡 MEDIUM - Generic positioning

🔍 Windows Event Log Recovery
Method 1: Built-in Windows Event Viewer
# Open Event Viewer and export logs
eventvwr.msc

# Or via PowerShell - get events from Oct 30, 2025
Get-WinEvent -FilterHashtable @{LogName='Security'; StartTime='10/30/2025'; EndTime='10/31/2025'} | Export-Csv "H:\security_logs_oct30.csv"

Get-WinEvent -FilterHashtable @{LogName='System'; StartTime='10/30/2025'; EndTime='10/31/2025'} | Export-Csv "H:\system_logs_oct30.csv"

Get-WinEvent -FilterHashtable @{LogName='Application'; StartTime='10/30/2025'; EndTime='10/31/2025'} | Export-Csv "H:\app_logs_oct30.csv"
Method 2: Scheduled Tasks History
# Get scheduled task history
Get-ScheduledTask | Get-ScheduledTaskInfo | Where-Object {$_.LastRunTime -like "*10/30/2025*"} | Export-Csv "H:\scheduled_tasks_oct30.csv"

# More detailed task history
schtasks /query /fo csv /v > "H:\all_scheduled_tasks.csv"
🕵️ Network and Access Logs
Method 3: Network Connection Logs
# Check network connections (if logs still exist)
netstat -an > "H:\network_connections.txt"

# Check routing table
route print > "H:\routing_table.txt"
Method 4: File Access Logs
# Check recent file access
Get-WinEvent -FilterHashtable @{LogName='Security'; ID=4663} | Where-Object {$_.TimeCreated -like "*10/30/2025*"} | Export-Csv "H:\file_access_oct30.csv"
🔧 Advanced Recovery Tools
Method 5: PowerShell History
# Check PowerShell command history
Get-Content (Get-PSReadlineOption).HistorySavePath | Out-File "H:\powershell_history.txt"
Method 6: Browser History Recovery
# Chrome history (if it exists)
Copy-Item "$env:LOCALAPPDATA\Google\Chrome\User Data\Default\History" "H:\chrome_history_backup.db"

# Edge history
Copy-Item "$env:LOCALAPPDATA\Microsoft\Edge\User Data\Default\History" "H:\edge_history_backup.db"
📊 Third-Party Forensic Tools
Method 7: Free Forensic Tools
Nirsoft Tools: Download WinLogOnView, BrowsingHistoryView, etc.
Sysinternals: Process Monitor, Process Explorer logs
Event Log Explorer: More detailed event analysis
Method 8: System Restore Points
# Check if system restore points exist from before Oct 30
Get-ComputerRestorePoint | Where-Object {$_.CreationTime -lt "10/30/2025"}

Git won’t install its own SSH binaries, so you’ll need to ensure your external SSH is properly configured. ✅ What You Should Choose Since you're setting up Git fresh on Windows and want a stable, predictable environment, sticking with the bundled OpenSSH is the safest choice. What are the different approaches to handle Windows permission errors when analyzing drives, and how can I safely bypass system folder restrictions for comprehensive storage analysis?

Office Agent
Office Agent
Great question! You're dealing with Windows permission restrictions when trying to analyze your drives. Let me explain the different approaches and provide you with safe solutions:

🔧 Approaches to Handle Windows Permission Errors
1. PowerShell with Error Handling (Recommended)
# Safe approach - skips protected folders
Get-ChildItem -Path "E:\" -Recurse -Force -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | 
Where-Object { 
    $_.FullName -notlike "*System Volume Information*" -and
    $_.FullName -notlike "*\$RECYCLE.BIN*" -and
    $_.FullName -notlike "*pagefile.sys*" -and
    $_.FullName -notlike "*hiberfil.sys*"
} |
Select-Object FullName, Length, LastWriteTime, @{Name="Type";Expression={if($_.PSIsContainer){"Folder"}else{"File"}}} | 
Export-Csv -Path "USB_Drive_E_Safe_Analysis.csv" -NoTypeInformation
2. Administrative PowerShell (More Comprehensive)
# Run PowerShell as Administrator first, then:
Get-ChildItem -Path "E:\" -Recurse -Force -ErrorAction Continue | 
Select-Object FullName, Length, LastWriteTime, @{Name="Type";Expression={if($_.PSIsContainer){"Folder"}else{"File"}}} | 
Export-Csv -Path "USB_Drive_E_Admin_Analysis.csv" -NoTypeInformation
3. Command Prompt Alternative
# Simple but effective
dir E:\ /s /a /-c > USB_Drive_E_Listing.txt
4. Robocopy for File Listing (Advanced)
# Creates detailed file list without copying
robocopy E:\ NUL /L /S /NJH /NJS /FP /NC /NDL /TS > USB_Drive_E_Robocopy.txt
🛡️ Safe Bypass Methods for System Restrictions
Method 1: Selective Exclusion (Safest)
$ExcludedPaths = @(
    "*System Volume Information*",
    "*\$RECYCLE.BIN*",
    "*pagefile.sys*",
    "*hiberfil.sys*",
    "*swapfile.sys*",
    "*DumpStack.log*"
)

Get-ChildItem -Path "E:\" -Recurse -Force -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | 
Where-Object { 
    $exclude = $false
    foreach ($pattern in $ExcludedPaths) {
        if ($_.FullName -like $pattern) {
            $exclude = $true
            break
        }
    }
    -not $exclude
} | 
Select-Object FullName, Length, LastWriteTime, @{Name="Type";Expression={if($_.PSIsContainer){"Folder"}else{"File"}}} | 
Export-Csv -Path "USB_Drive_E_Filtered.csv" -NoTypeInformation
Method 2: Try-Catch with Detailed Logging
$Results = @()
$ErrorLog = @()

function Get-SafeChildItems {
    param($Path)
    
    try {
        Get-ChildItem -Path $Path -Force | ForEach-Object {
            try {
                $item = $_
                $Results += [PSCustomObject]@{
                    FullName = $item.FullName
                    Length = if($item.PSIsContainer) { 0 } else { $item.Length }
                    LastWriteTime = $item.LastWriteTime
                    Type = if($item.PSIsContainer) { "Folder" } else { "File" }
                }
                
                if ($item.PSIsContainer) {
                    Get-SafeChildItems -Path $item.FullName
                }
            }
            catch {
                $ErrorLog += "Access denied: $($item.FullName)"
            }
        }
    }
    catch {
        $ErrorLog += "Cannot access: $Path"
    }
}

Get-SafeChildItems -Path "E:\"
$Results | Export-Csv -Path "USB_Drive_E_Safe.csv" -NoTypeInformation
$ErrorLog | Out-File -FilePath "USB_Drive_E_Errors.txt"

              @{Name="TotalSize_GB";Expression={[math]::Round($_.Size/1GB,2)}},
              @{Name="FreeSpace_GB";Expression={[math]::Round($_.FreeSpace/1GB,2)}},
              @{Name="UsedSpace_GB";Expression={[math]::Round(($_.Size-$_.FreeSpace)/1GB,2)}},
              @{Name="UsedPercent";Expression={[math]::Round((($_.Size-$_.FreeSpace)/$_.Size)*100,2)}} |
Format-Table -AutoSize

How does B85+GZIP compression compare to other compression methods for AI context encoding, and what are the trade-offs?

Office Agent
Office Agent
Great question! Let me analyze the compression performance and trade-offs of different encoding strategies used in your AI Context Orchestrator:


Reading file
encode_context.py
Excellent question! Let me analyze the compression strategies in your AI Context Orchestrator and compare their performance characteristics:


Executing command
python -c " import json import base64 import gzip # Test data - your compact AI instructions test_data = '''{\n \"workspace_overview\": \"Charles Kendrick's multi-project AI development workspace\",\n \"core_projects\": {\n \"ai_orchestrator\": {\n \"purpose\": \"Context injection & steganography for AI workflows\",\n \"key_files\": [\"encode_context.py\", \"decode_context.py\", \"cli.py\"],\n \"output_dir\": \"Whisper_Deck/\",\n \"pattern\": \"JSON extraction → compression → PNG steganography\"\n }\n }\n}''' raw_bytes = test_data.encode('utf-8') gzip_bytes = gzip.compress(raw_bytes) print('📊 COMPRESSION ANALYSIS') print('=' * 50) print(f'Original JSON: {len(raw_bytes)} bytes') print(f'GZIP compressed: {len(gzip_bytes)} bytes ({len(gzip_bytes)/len(raw_bytes)*100:.1f}%)') print() # Strategy 1: B64+JSON b64_json = base64.b64encode(raw_bytes).decode('ascii') print(f'B64+JSON: {len(b64_json)} chars ({len(b64_json)/len(raw_bytes)*100:.1f}% overhead)') # Strategy 2: B64+GZIP+JSON b64_gzip = base64.b64encode(gzip_bytes).decode('ascii') print(f'B64+GZIP+JSON: {len(b64_gzip)} chars ({len(b64_gzip)/len(raw_bytes)*100:.1f}% vs original)') # Strategy 3: B85+GZIP+JSON b85_gzip = base64.a85encode(gzip_bytes, adobe=False).decode('ascii') print(f'B85+GZIP+JSON: {len(b85_gzip)} chars ({len(b85_gzip)/len(raw_bytes)*100:.1f}% vs original)') print() print('🏆 WINNER ANALYSIS:') strategies = { 'B64+JSON': len(b64_json), 'B64+GZIP+JSON': len(b64_gzip), 'B85+GZIP+JSON': len(b85_gzip) } winner = min(strategies.items(), key=lambda x: x[1]) print(f'Smallest: {winner[0]} at {winner[1]} characters') print() print('💾 SIZE COMPARISON:') for name, size in sorted(strategies.items(), key=lambda x: x[1]): savings = (1 - size/len(raw_bytes)) * 100 print(f'{name:15} {size:4d} chars ({savings:+5.1f}% vs raw)') "
Perfect! Now let me analyze the compression performance with your actual Manus interaction data:


Executing command
python -c " import json import base64 import gzip import os # Read the Manus analysis file with open('manus_interaction_analysis.json', 'r') as f: data = f.read() raw_bytes = data.encode('utf-8') gzip_bytes = gzip.compress(raw_bytes) print('📊 MANUS DATA COMPRESSION ANALYSIS') print('=' * 60) print(f'Original JSON: {len(raw_bytes):,} bytes') print(f'GZIP compressed: {len(gzip_bytes):,} bytes ({len(gzip_bytes)/len(raw_bytes)*100:.1f}%)') print() # Strategy comparison strategies = {} # B64+JSON b64_json = base64.b64encode(raw_bytes).decode('ascii') strategies['B64+JSON'] = len(b64_json) # B64+GZIP+JSON b64_gzip = base64.b64encode(gzip_bytes).decode('ascii') strategies['B64+GZIP+JSON'] = len(b64_gzip) # B85+GZIP+JSON b85_gzip = base64.a85encode(gzip_bytes, adobe=False).decode('ascii') strategies['B85+GZIP+JSON'] = len(b85_gzip) print('🏆 COMPRESSION RESULTS:') for name, size in sorted(strategies.items(), key=lambda x: x[1]): compression_ratio = size / len(raw_bytes) savings = (1 - compression_ratio) * 100 print(f'{name:15} {size:4d} chars ({compression_ratio:.2f}x, {savings:+5.1f}%)') print() print('🎯 AI INSTRUCTION LIMITS:') for name, size in strategies.items(): status = '✅ FITS' if size <= 2000 else '❌ TOO BIG' print(f'{name:15} {size:4d}/2000 chars {status}') print() print('⚡ PERFORMANCE INSIGHTS:') print(f'• GZIP reduces raw data by {(1-len(gzip_bytes)/len(raw_bytes))*100:.1f}%') print(f'• B85 encoding is {(len(b64_gzip)-len(b85_gzip))/len(b64_gzip)*100:.1f}% smaller than B64') print(f'• Best strategy saves {(1-min(strategies.values())/len(raw_bytes))*100:.1f}% vs raw JSON') "
